Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 72, the first release of the Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) Command Module (CM) software for Apollo 13.

They have been adapted from sources files created from a listing of Comanche 55. These source files were updated to match binary dumps of a set of Comanche 67 rope modules. They were then further modified by applying known changes between Comanche 67 and Comanche 72. A binary dump of module B2 of Comanche 72, part number 2010802-021, was also used to validate changes made to banks 05-13. The resulting code assembles to have identical memory-bank checksums as those specified in NASA drawing 2021153G; this gives reasonably high confidence that the changes that have been made are correct. In places where ambiguity exists, this ambiguity is discussed in "## Reconstruction:" comments.

Since no contemporary listings of Comanche 72 are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

001502,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
001503,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    ERASABLE_ASSIGNMENTS.agc
001504,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Comanche revision 072.
001505,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the first
001506,000006:                                                                                                  ##              release of the software for the Command Module's (CM) Apollo
001507,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13. No original listings
001508,000008:                                                                                                  ##              of this program are available; instead, this file was recreated
001509,000009:                                                                                                  ##              from a printout of Comanche 055, binary dumps of a set of
001510,000010:                                                                                                  ##              Comanche 067 rope modules, and changelogs between Comanche 067
001511,000011:                                                                                                  ##              and 072. It has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
001512,000012:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Comanche 072 in NASA drawing
001513,000013:                                                                                                  ##              2021153G, which gives relatively high confidence that the
001514,000014:                                                                                                  ##              reconstruction is correct.
001515,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
001516,000016:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
001517,000017:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
001518,000018:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2024-05-13 MAS  Created from Comanche 067.
001519,000019:                                                                                                  ##              2024-05-14 MAS  Implemented fix for COM-21, "Backwards
001520,000020:                                                                                                  ##                              integration can occur in P27 uplink".
001521,000021:                                                                                                  ##              2024-05-16 MAS  Implemented PCR-936.1, "Initialize V90 time
001522,000022:                                                                                                  ##                              to TIG".
001523,000023: 
001524,000024:                                                                                                  #  CONVENTIONS AND NOTATIONS UTILIZED FOR ERASABLE ASSIGNMENTS.
001525,000025: 
001526,000026:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  IS USED IN TWO WAYS.  IT IS OFTEN USED TO CHAIN A GROUP
001527,000027:                                                                                                  #                OF ASSIGNMENTS SO THAT THE GROUP MAY BE MOVED WITH THE
001528,000028:                                                                                                  #                CHANGING OF ONLY ONE CARD.  EXAMPLE.
001529,000029: 
001530,000030:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  START
001531,000031:                                                                                                  #                        Y       EQUALS  X       +SIZE.X
001532,000032:                                                                                                  #                        Z       EQUALS  Y       +SIZE.Y
001533,000033: 
001534,000034:                                                                                                  #                (X, Y, AND Z ARE CONSECUTIVE AND BEGIN AT START.       )
001535,000035:                                                                                                  #                (SIZE.X AND SIZE.Y ARE THE RESPECTIVE SIZES OF X AND Y,
001536,000036:                                                                                                  #                 USUALLY NUMERIC, IE. 1, 2, 6, 18D ETC.                )
001537,000037: 
001538,000038:                                                                                                  #        EQUALS  OFTEN IMPLIES THE SHARING OF REGISTERS (DIFFERENT NAMES
001539,000039:                                                                                                  #                AND DIFFERENT DATA).  EXAMPLE.
001540,000040: 
001541,000041:                                                                                                  #                        X       EQUALS  Y
001542,000042: 
001543,000043:                                                                                                  #        =       MEANS THAT MULTIPLE NAMES HAVE BEEN GIVEN TO THE SAME DATA.
001544,000044:                                                                                                  #                (THIS IS LOGICAL EQUIVALENCE, NOT SHARING)  EXAMPLE.
001545,000045: 
001546,000046:                                                                                                  #                        X       =       Y
001547,000047: 
001548,000048:                                                                                                  #        THE SIZE AND UTILIZATION OF AN ERASABLE ARE OFTEN INCLUDED IN
001549,000049:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMENTS IN THE FOLLOWING FORM.  M(SIZE)N.
001550,000050: 
001551,000051:                                                                                                  #                M       REFERS TO THE MOBILITY OF THE ASSIGNMENT.
001552,000052:                                                                                                  #                        B       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED BY BASIC
001553,000053:                                                                                                  #                                INSTRUCTIONS AND THUS IS E-BANK SENSITIVE.
001554,000054:                                                                                                  #                        I       MEANS THAT THE SYMBOL IS REFERENCED ONLY BY
001555,000055:                                                                                                  #                                INTERPRETIVE INSTRUCTIONS, AND IS THUS E-BANK
001556,000056:                                                                                                  #                                INSENSITIVE AND MAY APPEAR IN ANY E-BANK.
001557,000057: 
001558,000058:                                                                                                  #                SIZE    IS THE NUMBER OF REGISTERS INCLUDED BY THE SYMBOL.
001559,000059: 
001560,000060:                                                                                                  #                N       INDICATES THE NATURE OR PERMANENCE OF THE CONTENTS.
001561,000061:                                                                                                  #                        PL      MEANS THAT THE CONTENTS ARE PAD LOADED.
001562,000062:                                                                                                  #                        DSP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED FOR A DISPLAY.
001563,000063:                                                                                                  #                        PRM     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS PERMANENT, IE. IT
001564,000064:                                                                                                  #                                IS USED DURING THE ENTIRE MISSION FOR ONE
001565,000065:                                                                                                  #                                PURPOSE AND CANNOT BE SHARED.
001566,000066:                                                                                                  #                        TMP     MEANS THAT THE REGISTER IS USED TEMPORARILY OR
001567,000067:                                                                                                  #                                IS A SCRATCH REGISTER FOR THE ROUTINE TO WHICH
001568,000068:                                                                                                  #                                IT IS ASSIGNED.  THAT IS, IT NEED NOT BE SET
001569,000069:                                                                                                  #                                PRIOR TO INVOCATION OF THE ROUTINE NOR DOES IT
001570,000070:                                                                                                  #                                CONTAIN USEFUL OUTPUT TO ANOTHER ROUTINE.  THUS
001571,000071:                                                                                                  #                                IT MAY BE SHARED WITH ANY OTHER ROUTINE WHICH
001572,000072:                                                                                                  #                                IS NOT ACTIVE IN PARALLEL.
001573,000073:                                                                                                  #                        IN      MEANS INPUT TO THE ROUTINE AND IT IS PROBABLY
001574,000074:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001575,000075:                                                                                                  #                        OUT     MEANS OUTPUT FROM THE ROUTINE, PROBABLY
001576,000076:                                                                                                  #                                TEMPORARY FOR A HIGHER-LEVEL ROUTINE/PROGRAM.
001577,000077: 
001578,000078: 
001579,000079:                                                                                                  #  SPECIAL REGISTERS.
001580,000080: 
001581,000081: 37,2001                        A                  EQUALS   0                                     
001582,000082: 37,2001                        L                  EQUALS   1                                     #  L AND Q ARE BOTH CHANNELS AND REGISTERS.
001583,000083: 37,2001                        Q                  EQUALS   2                                     
001584,000084: 37,2001                        EBANK              EQUALS   3                                     
001585,000085: 37,2001                        FBANK              EQUALS   4                                     
001586,000086: 37,2001                        Z                  EQUALS   5                                     #  ADJACENT TO FBANK AND BBANK FOR DXCH Z
001587,000087: 37,2001                        BBANK              EQUALS   6                                     #  (DTCB) AND DXCH FBANK (DTCF).
001588,000088:                                                                                                  #  REGISTER 7 IS A ZERO-SOURCE, USED BY ZL.
001589,000089: 
001590,000090: 37,2001                        ARUPT              EQUALS   10                                    #  INTERRUPT STORAGE.
001591,000091: 37,2001                        LRUPT              EQUALS   11                                    
001592,000092: 37,2001                        QRUPT              EQUALS   12                                    
001593,000093: 37,2001                        SAMPTIME           EQUALS   13                                    #  SAMPLED TIME 1 & 2.
001594,000094: 37,2001                        ZRUPT              EQUALS   15                                    #  (13 AND 14 ARE SPARES.)
001595,000095: 37,2001                        BANKRUPT           EQUALS   16                                    #  USUALLY HOLDS FBANK OR BBANK.
001596,000096: 37,2001                        BRUPT              EQUALS   17                                    #  RESUME ADDRESS AS WELL.
001597,000097: 
001598,000098: 37,2001                        CYR                EQUALS   20                                    
001599,000099: 37,2001                        SR                 EQUALS   21                                    
001600,000100: 37,2001                        CYL                EQUALS   22                                    
001601,000101: 37,2001                        EDOP               EQUALS   23                                    #  EDITS INTERPRETIVE OPERATION CODE PAIRS.

001628,000128: 
001629,000129: 
001630,000130: 37,2001                        CDUZCMD            EQUALS   52                                    
001631,000131: 37,2001                        CDUTCMD            EQUALS   53                                    #  OPTICS TRUNNION COMMAND (WAS OPTYCMD).
001632,000132: 37,2001  0000053               OPTYCMD            =        CDUTCMD                               
001633,000133: 37,2001  0000053               TVCYAW             EQUALS   CDUTCMD                               #  SPS YAW COMMAND IN TVC MODE.

001635,000135: 37,2001  0000054               TVCPITCH           EQUALS   CDUSCMD                               #  SPS PITCH COMMAND IN TVC MODE.
001636,000136: 37,2001  0000054               OPTXCMD            =        CDUSCMD                               
001637,000137: 37,2001                        EMSD               EQUALS   55                                    
001638,000138: 37,2001                        THRUST             EQUALS   55

001646,000146: 37,2001                        LV                 EQUALS   36D                                   #  LENGTH OF VECTOR INPUT TO UNIT.

002909,001409: 
002910,001410:    0061                                           SETLOC   61                                    
002911,001411:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT TEMPORARY STORAGE POOL.     (11D)
002912,001412: 
002913,001413:                                                                                                  #  (ITEMP1 THROUGH RUPTREG4)             
002914,001414: 
002915,001415:                                                                                                  #  ANY OF THESE MAY BE USED AS TEMPORARIES DURING INTERRUPT OR WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED. THE ITEMP SERIES
002916,001416:                                                                                                  #  IS USED DURING CALLS TO THE EXECUTIVE AND WAITLIST - THE RUPTREGS ARE NOT.
002917,001417: 
002918,001418:    0061                        ITEMP1             ERASE                                          
002919,001419:    0062     0061               WAITEXIT           EQUALS   ITEMP1                                
002920,001420:    0062     0061               EXECTEM1           EQUALS   ITEMP1                                
002921,001421: 
002922,001422:    0062                        ITEMP2             ERASE                                          
002923,001423:    0063     0062               WAITBANK           EQUALS   ITEMP2                                
002924,001424:    0063     0062               EXECTEM2           EQUALS   ITEMP2                                
002925,001425: 
002926,001426:    0063                        ITEMP3             ERASE                                          
002927,001427:    0064     0063               RUPTSTOR           EQUALS   ITEMP3                                
002928,001428:    0064     0063               WAITADR            EQUALS   ITEMP3                                
002929,001429:    0064     0063               NEWPRIO            EQUALS   ITEMP3                                
002930,001430: 
002931,001431:    0064                        ITEMP4             ERASE                                          
002932,001432:    0065     0064               LOCCTR             EQUALS   ITEMP4                                
002933,001433:    0065     0064               WAITTEMP           EQUALS   ITEMP4                                
002934,001434: 
002935,001435:    0065                        ITEMP5             ERASE                                          
002936,001436:    0066     0065               NEWLOC             EQUALS   ITEMP5                                
002937,001437: 
002938,001438:    0066                        ITEMP6             ERASE                                          
002939,001439:                                                                                                  #  NEWLOC+1      EQUALS  ITEMP6          DP ADDRESS.
002940,001440: 
002941,001441:    0067                                           SETLOC   67                                    
002942,001442:    0067                        NEWJOB             ERASE                                          #  MUST BE AT LOC 67 DUE TO WIRING.
002943,001443: 
002944,001444:    0070                        RUPTREG1           ERASE                                          
002945,001445:    0071                        RUPTREG2           ERASE                                          
002946,001446:    0072                        RUPTREG3           ERASE                                          
002947,001447:    0073                        RUPTREG4           ERASE                                          
002948,001448:    0074     0073               KEYTEMP1           EQUALS   RUPTREG4                              
002949,001449:    0074     0073               DSRUPTEM           EQUALS   RUPTREG4                              
002950,001450: 
002951,001451:                                                                                                  #  FLAGWORD RESERVATIONS.                (12D)
002952,001452: 
002953,001453:    0074                        STATE              ERASE    +11D                                  
002954,001454: 
002955,001455:                                                                                                  #  PAD LOAD FOR DAPS                     (1)
002956,001456: 
002957,001457:    0110                        EMDOT              ERASE                                          #  I(1)PL SPS FLOW RATE, SC. AT B+3 KG/CS
002958,001458:

002960,001460:                                                                                                  #  OPTION FOR V82                        (1D)
002961,001461:    0111                        OPTION82           ERASE                                          #  B(1)
002962,001462: 
002963,001463:                                                                                                  #  UNUSED ERASABLES ********(2)
002964,001464:    0112                        ERASFILL           ERASE    +1                                    
002965,001465: 
002966,001466:                                                                                                  #  EXEC TEMPORARIES WHICH MAY BE USED BETWEEN CCS NEWJOBS.
002967,001467:                                                                                                  #  (INTB15+ THROUGH RUPTMXM)             (32D)
002968,001468:    0114                        INTB15+            ERASE                                          #  REFLECTS 15TH BIT OF INDEXABLE ADDRESSES
002969,001469:    0115     0114               DSEXIT             EQUALS   INTB15+                               #  RETURN FOR DSPIN
002970,001470:    0115     0114               EXITEM             EQUALS   INTB15+                               #  RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
002971,001471:    0115     0114               BLANKRET           EQUALS   INTB15+                               #  RETURN FOR 2BLANK
002972,001472: 
002973,001473:    0115                        INTBIT15           ERASE                                          #  SIMILAR TO ABOVE.
002974,001474:    0116     0115               WRDRET             EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR 5BLANK
002975,001475:    0116     0115               WDRET              EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR DSPWD
002976,001476:    0116     0115               DECRET             EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
002977,001477:    0116     0115               21/22REG           EQUALS   INTBIT15                              #  TEMP FOR CHARIN
002978,001478: 
002979,001479:                                                                                                  #  THE REGISTERS BETWEEN ADDRWD AND PRIORITY MUST STAY IN THE FOLLOWING ORDER FOR INTERPRETIVE TRACE.
002980,001480: 
002981,001481:    0116                        ADDRWD             ERASE                                          #  12 BIT INTERPRETIVE OPERAND SUB-ADDRESS.
002982,001482:    0117                        POLISH             ERASE                                          #  HOLDS CADR MADE FROM POLISH ADDRESS.
002983,001483:    0120     0117               UPDATRET           EQUALS   POLISH                                #  RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
002984,001484:    0120     0117               CHAR               EQUALS   POLISH                                #  TEMP FOR CHARIN
002985,001485:    0120     0117               ERCNT              EQUALS   POLISH                                #  COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
